{\footnotesize\ttfamily typedef int32\+\_\+t \mbox{\hyperlink{namespacepros_1_1c_a819f455cfd280a0a3f2489ee88aa19ac}{ext\+\_\+adi\+\_\+encoder\+\_\+t}}}



Reference type for an initialized encoder. 

This merely contains the port number for the encoder, unlike its use as an object to store encoder data in P\+R\+OS 2. \mbox{\Hypertarget{namespacepros_1_1c_a628d2ba74a77b5d590e4b865e3f4a7aa}\label{namespacepros_1_1c_a628d2ba74a77b5d590e4b865e3f4a7aa}}

Get the currently measured distance from the sensor in mm. 

This function uses the following values of errno when an error state is reached\+: E\+N\+X\+IO -\/ The given value is not within the range of V5 ports (1-\/21). E\+N\+O\+D\+EV -\/ The port cannot be configured as an \mbox{\hyperlink{classpros_1_1Distance}{Distance}} Sensor

\hline
\end{DoxyParams}

\end{DoxyReturn}
\mbox{\Hypertarget{namespacepros_1_1c_a97b69852b0f1ec60cdac10ca20caabdc}\label{namespacepros_1_1c_a97b69852b0f1ec60cdac10ca20caabdc}} 
\index{pros::c@{pros::c}!distance\_get\_confidence@{distance\_get\_confidence}}
\index{distance\_get\_confidence@{distance\_get\_confidence}!pros::c@{pros::c}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{distance\_get\_confidence()}{distance\_get\_confidence()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily int32\+\_\+t pros\+::c\+::distance\+\_\+get\+\_\+confidence (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{uint8\+\_\+t}]{port }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Get the confidence in the distance reading. 

This is a value that has a range of 0 to 63. 63 means high confidence, lower values imply less confidence. Confidence is only available when distance is $>$ 200mm (the value 10 is returned in this scenario).

This function uses the following values of errno when an error state is reached\+: E\+N\+X\+IO -\/ The given value is not within the range of V5 ports (1-\/21). E\+N\+O\+D\+EV -\/ The port cannot be configured as an \mbox{\hyperlink{classpros_1_1Distance}{Distance}} Sensor


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em port} & The V5 \mbox{\hyperlink{classpros_1_1Distance}{Distance}} Sensor port number from 1-\/21 \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
The confidence value or P\+R\+O\+S\+\_\+\+E\+RR if the operation failed, setting errno. 
\end{DoxyReturn}

Get the current guess at relative object size. 

This is a value that has a range of 0 to 400. A 18\char`\"{} x 30\char`\"{} grey card will return a value of approximately 75 in typical room lighting.

These functions allow for interaction with any A\+DI port type ~\newline

This function uses the following values of errno when an error state is reached\+: E\+N\+X\+IO -\/ Either the A\+DI port value or the smart port value is not within its valid range (A\+DI port\+: 1-\/8, \textquotesingle{}a\textquotesingle{}-\/\textquotesingle{}h\textquotesingle{}, or \textquotesingle{}A\textquotesingle{}-\/\textquotesingle{}H\textquotesingle{}; smart port\+: 1-\/21).

\mbox{\Hypertarget{namespacepros_1_1c_ac7ce5918ef247fbfbebadb8b87417ced}\label{namespacepros_1_1c_ac7ce5918ef247fbfbebadb8b87417ced}} 
\index{pros::c@{pros::c}!ext\_adi\_analog\_calibrate@{ext\_adi\_analog\_calibrate}}
\index{ext\_adi\_analog\_calibrate@{ext\_adi\_analog\_calibrate}!pros::c@{pros::c}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{ext\_adi\_analog\_calibrate()}{ext\_adi\_analog\_calibrate()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily int32\+\_\+t pros\+::c\+::ext\+\_\+adi\+\_\+analog\+\_\+calibrate (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{uint8\+\_\+t}]{smart\+\_\+port,  }\item[{uint8\+\_\+t}]{adi\+\_\+port }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Calibrates the analog sensor on the specified port and returns the new calibration value. 

This method assumes that the true sensor value is not actively changing at this time and computes an average from approximately 500 samples, 1 ms apart, for a 0.\+5 s period of calibration. The average value thus calculated is returned and stored for later calls to the \mbox{\hyperlink{group__c-adi_ga34a3205b4beecc2efb561a068ac869e7}{adi\+\_\+analog\+\_\+read\+\_\+calibrated()}} and \mbox{\hyperlink{group__c-adi_ga0a62ec5516d617b8282f9f1c21e68e15}{adi\+\_\+analog\+\_\+read\+\_\+calibrated\+\_\+\+H\+R()}} functions. These functions will return the difference between this value and the current sensor value when called.

Do not use this function when the sensor value might be unstable (gyro rotation, accelerometer movement).

This function uses the following values of errno when an error state is reached\+: E\+N\+X\+IO -\/ Either the A\+DI port value or the smart port value is not within its valid range (A\+DI port\+: 1-\/8, \textquotesingle{}a\textquotesingle{}-\/\textquotesingle{}h\textquotesingle{}, or \textquotesingle{}A\textquotesingle{}-\/\textquotesingle{}H\textquotesingle{}; smart port\+: 1-\/21).


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em smart\+\_\+port} & The smart port number that the A\+DI Expander is in \\
\hline
{\em adi\+\_\+port} & The A\+DI port to calibrate (from 1-\/8, \textquotesingle{}a\textquotesingle{}-\/\textquotesingle{}h\textquotesingle{}, \textquotesingle{}A\textquotesingle{}-\/\textquotesingle{}H\textquotesingle{})\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
The average sensor value computed by this function 
\end{DoxyReturn}
\mbox{\Hypertarget{namespacepros_1_1c_ad23c527e73c2008d5bf49030efa255ef}\label{namespacepros_1_1c_ad23c527e73c2008d5bf49030efa255ef}} 
\index{pros::c@{pros::c}!ext\_adi\_analog\_read@{ext\_adi\_analog\_read}}
\index{ext\_adi\_analog\_read@{ext\_adi\_analog\_read}!pros::c@{pros::c}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{ext\_adi\_analog\_read()}{ext\_adi\_analog\_read()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily int32\+\_\+t pros\+::c\+::ext\+\_\+adi\+\_\+analog\+\_\+read (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{uint8\+\_\+t}]{smart\+\_\+port,  }\item[{uint8\+\_\+t}]{adi\+\_\+port }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Gets the 12-\/bit value of the specified port. 

The value returned is undefined if the analog pin has been switched to a different mode.

This function uses the following values of errno when an error state is reached\+: E\+N\+X\+IO -\/ Either the A\+DI port value or the smart port value is not within its valid range (A\+DI port\+: 1-\/8, \textquotesingle{}a\textquotesingle{}-\/\textquotesingle{}h\textquotesingle{}, or \textquotesingle{}A\textquotesingle{}-\/\textquotesingle{}H\textquotesingle{}; smart port\+: 1-\/21). E\+A\+D\+D\+R\+I\+N\+U\+SE -\/ The port is not configured as an analog input


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em smart\+\_\+port} & The smart port number that the A\+DI Expander is in \\
\hline
{\em adi\+\_\+port} & The A\+DI port (from 1-\/8, \textquotesingle{}a\textquotesingle{}-\/\textquotesingle{}h\textquotesingle{}, \textquotesingle{}A\textquotesingle{}-\/\textquotesingle{}H\textquotesingle{}) for which the value will be returned\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
The analog sensor value, where a value of 0 reflects an input voltage of nearly 0 V and a value of 4095 reflects an input voltage of nearly 5 V 
\end{DoxyReturn}
\mbox{\Hypertarget{namespacepros_1_1c_a2dd9e7a9e761ed80088bcf7f44920a42}\label{namespacepros_1_1c_a2dd9e7a9e761ed80088bcf7f44920a42}} 
\index{pros::c@{pros::c}!ext\_adi\_analog\_read\_calibrated@{ext\_adi\_analog\_read\_calibrated}}
\index{ext\_adi\_analog\_read\_calibrated@{ext\_adi\_analog\_read\_calibrated}!pros::c@{pros::c}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{ext\_adi\_analog\_read\_calibrated()}{ext\_adi\_analog\_read\_calibrated()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily int32\+\_\+t pros\+::c\+::ext\+\_\+adi\+\_\+analog\+\_\+read\+\_\+calibrated (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{uint8\+\_\+t}]{smart\+\_\+port,  }\item[{uint8\+\_\+t}]{adi\+\_\+port }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Gets the 12 bit calibrated value of an analog input port. 

The \mbox{\hyperlink{group__c-adi_gadebbf89bed5c3464bd77712c4c53edef}{adi\+\_\+analog\+\_\+calibrate()}} function must be run first. This function is inappropriate for sensor values intended for integration, as round-\/off error can accumulate causing drift over time. Use \mbox{\hyperlink{group__c-adi_ga0a62ec5516d617b8282f9f1c21e68e15}{adi\+\_\+analog\+\_\+read\+\_\+calibrated\+\_\+\+H\+R()}} instead.

This function uses the following values of errno when an error state is reached\+: E\+N\+X\+IO -\/ Either the A\+DI port value or the smart port value is not within its valid range (A\+DI port\+: 1-\/8, \textquotesingle{}a\textquotesingle{}-\/\textquotesingle{}h\textquotesingle{}, or \textquotesingle{}A\textquotesingle{}-\/\textquotesingle{}H\textquotesingle{}; smart port\+: 1-\/21). E\+A\+D\+D\+R\+I\+N\+U\+SE -\/ The port is not configured as an analog input


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em smart\+\_\+port} & The smart port number that the A\+DI Expander is in \\
\hline
{\em adi\+\_\+port} & The A\+DI port (from 1-\/8, \textquotesingle{}a\textquotesingle{}-\/\textquotesingle{}h\textquotesingle{}, \textquotesingle{}A\textquotesingle{}-\/\textquotesingle{}H\textquotesingle{}) for which the value will be returned\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
The difference of the sensor value from its calibrated default from -\/4095 to 4095 
\end{DoxyReturn}
\mbox{\Hypertarget{namespacepros_1_1c_a4e1d85f2e166adf83743b9fde5c504e8}\label{namespacepros_1_1c_a4e1d85f2e166adf83743b9fde5c504e8}} 
\index{pros::c@{pros::c}!ext\_adi\_analog\_read\_calibrated\_HR@{ext\_adi\_analog\_read\_calibrated\_HR}}
\index{ext\_adi\_analog\_read\_calibrated\_HR@{ext\_adi\_analog\_read\_calibrated\_HR}!pros::c@{pros::c}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{ext\_adi\_analog\_read\_calibrated\_HR()}{ext\_adi\_analog\_read\_calibrated\_HR()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily int32\+\_\+t pros\+::c\+::ext\+\_\+adi\+\_\+analog\+\_\+read\+\_\+calibrated\+\_\+\+HR (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{uint8\+\_\+t}]{smart\+\_\+port,  }\item[{uint8\+\_\+t}]{adi\+\_\+port }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Gets the 16 bit calibrated value of an analog input port. 

The \mbox{\hyperlink{group__c-adi_gadebbf89bed5c3464bd77712c4c53edef}{adi\+\_\+analog\+\_\+calibrate()}} function must be run first. This is intended for integrated sensor values such as gyros and accelerometers to reduce drift due to round-\/off, and should not be used on a sensor such as a line tracker or potentiometer.

The value returned actually has 16 bits of \char`\"{}precision\char`\"{}, even though the A\+DC only reads 12 bits, so that error induced by the average value being between two values when integrated over time is trivial. Think of the value as the true value times 16.

This function uses the following values of errno when an error state is reached\+: E\+N\+X\+IO -\/ Either the A\+DI port value or the smart port value is not within its valid range (A\+DI port\+: 1-\/8, \textquotesingle{}a\textquotesingle{}-\/\textquotesingle{}h\textquotesingle{}, or \textquotesingle{}A\textquotesingle{}-\/\textquotesingle{}H\textquotesingle{}; smart port\+: 1-\/21). E\+A\+D\+D\+R\+I\+N\+U\+SE -\/ The port is not configured as an analog input


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em smart\+\_\+port} & The smart port number that the A\+DI Expander is in \\
\hline
{\em adi\+\_\+port} & The A\+DI port (from 1-\/8, \textquotesingle{}a\textquotesingle{}-\/\textquotesingle{}h\textquotesingle{}, \textquotesingle{}A\textquotesingle{}-\/\textquotesingle{}H\textquotesingle{}) for which the value will be returned\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
The difference of the sensor value from its calibrated default from -\/16384 to 16384 
\end{DoxyReturn}
\mbox{\Hypertarget{namespacepros_1_1c_ad030dfc04f9d5adb0861f940472974f0}\label{namespacepros_1_1c_ad030dfc04f9d5adb0861f940472974f0}} 
\index{pros::c@{pros::c}!ext\_adi\_digital\_read@{ext\_adi\_digital\_read}}
\index{ext\_adi\_digital\_read@{ext\_adi\_digital\_read}!pros::c@{pros::c}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{ext\_adi\_digital\_read()}{ext\_adi\_digital\_read()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily int32\+\_\+t pros\+::c\+::ext\+\_\+adi\+\_\+digital\+\_\+read (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{uint8\+\_\+t}]{smart\+\_\+port,  }\item[{uint8\+\_\+t}]{adi\+\_\+port }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Gets the digital value (1 or 0) of a port configured as a digital input. 

If the port is configured as some other mode, the digital value which reflects the current state of the port is returned, which may or may not differ from the currently set value. The return value is undefined for ports configured as any mode other than a Digital Input.

This function uses the following values of errno when an error state is reached\+: E\+N\+X\+IO -\/ Either the A\+DI port value or the smart port value is not within its valid range (A\+DI port\+: 1-\/8, \textquotesingle{}a\textquotesingle{}-\/\textquotesingle{}h\textquotesingle{}, or \textquotesingle{}A\textquotesingle{}-\/\textquotesingle{}H\textquotesingle{}; smart port\+: 1-\/21). E\+A\+D\+D\+R\+I\+N\+U\+SE -\/ The port is not configured as a digital input


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em smart\+\_\+port} & The smart port number that the A\+DI Expander is in \\
\hline
{\em adi\+\_\+port} & The A\+DI port to read (from 1-\/8, \textquotesingle{}a\textquotesingle{}-\/\textquotesingle{}h\textquotesingle{}, \textquotesingle{}A\textquotesingle{}-\/\textquotesingle{}H\textquotesingle{})\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
True if the pin is H\+I\+GH, or false if it is L\+OW 
\end{DoxyReturn}
\mbox{\Hypertarget{namespacepros_1_1c_ac5b25457c1f1277dd545b6fab326299c}\label{namespacepros_1_1c_ac5b25457c1f1277dd545b6fab326299c}} 
\index{pros::c@{pros::c}!ext\_adi\_digital\_get\_new\_press@{ext\_adi\_digital\_get\_new\_press}}
\index{ext\_adi\_digital\_get\_new\_press@{ext\_adi\_digital\_get\_new\_press}!pros::c@{pros::c}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{ext\_adi\_digital\_get\_new\_press()}{ext\_adi\_digital\_get\_new\_press()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily int32\+\_\+t pros\+::c\+::ext\+\_\+adi\+\_\+digital\+\_\+get\+\_\+new\+\_\+press (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{uint8\+\_\+t}]{smart\+\_\+port,  }\item[{uint8\+\_\+t}]{adi\+\_\+port }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Gets a rising-\/edge case for a digital button press. 

This function is not thread-\/safe. Multiple tasks polling a single button may return different results under the same circumstances, so only one task should call this function for any given button. E.\+g., \mbox{\hyperlink{classpros_1_1Task}{Task}} A calls this function for buttons 1 and 2. \mbox{\hyperlink{classpros_1_1Task}{Task}} B may call this function for button 3, but should not for buttons 1 or 2. A typical use-\/case for this function is to call inside opcontrol to detect new button presses, and not in any other tasks.

This function uses the following values of errno when an error state is reached\+: E\+N\+X\+IO -\/ Either the A\+DI port value or the smart port value is not within its valid range (A\+DI port\+: 1-\/8, \textquotesingle{}a\textquotesingle{}-\/\textquotesingle{}h\textquotesingle{}, or \textquotesingle{}A\textquotesingle{}-\/\textquotesingle{}H\textquotesingle{}; smart port\+: 1-\/21). E\+A\+D\+D\+R\+I\+N\+U\+SE -\/ The port is not configured as a digital input


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em smart\+\_\+port} & The smart port number that the A\+DI Expander is in \\
\hline
{\em adi\+\_\+port} & The A\+DI port to read (from 1-\/8, \textquotesingle{}a\textquotesingle{}-\/\textquotesingle{}h\textquotesingle{}, \textquotesingle{}A\textquotesingle{}-\/\textquotesingle{}H\textquotesingle{})\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
1 if the button is pressed and had not been pressed the last time this function was called, 0 otherwise. 
\end{DoxyReturn}
\mbox{\Hypertarget{namespacepros_1_1c_a638e7d47bbdde4b545be396d4cb20eea}\label{namespacepros_1_1c_a638e7d47bbdde4b545be396d4cb20eea}}

{\footnotesize\ttfamily int32\+\_\+t pros\+::c\+::ext\+\_\+adi\+\_\+encoder\+\_\+shutdown (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{namespacepros_1_1c_a819f455cfd280a0a3f2489ee88aa19ac}{ext\+\_\+adi\+\_\+encoder\+\_\+t}}}]{enc }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Disables the encoder and voids the configuration on its ports. 

This function uses the following values of errno when an error state is reached\+: E\+N\+X\+IO -\/ Either the A\+DI port value or the smart port value is not within its valid range (A\+DI port\+: 1-\/8, \textquotesingle{}a\textquotesingle{}-\/\textquotesingle{}h\textquotesingle{}, or \textquotesingle{}A\textquotesingle{}-\/\textquotesingle{}H\textquotesingle{}; smart port\+: 1-\/21). \hline
\end{DoxyParams}

\index{pros::c@{pros::c}!ext\_adi\_ultrasonic\_get@{ext\_adi\_ultrasonic\_get}}

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{ext\_adi\_ultrasonic\_get()}{ext\_adi\_ultrasonic\_get()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily int32\+\_\+t pros\+::c\+::ext\+\_\+adi\+\_\+ultrasonic\+\_\+get (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{namespacepros_1_1c_a628d2ba74a77b5d590e4b865e3f4a7aa}{ext\+\_\+adi\+\_\+ultrasonic\+\_\+t}}}]{ult }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Gets the current ultrasonic sensor value in centimeters. 

If no object was found, zero is returned. If the ultrasonic sensor was never started, the return value is undefined. Round and fluffy objects can cause inaccurate values to be returned.

This function uses the following values of errno when an error state is reached\+: E\+N\+X\+IO -\/ Either the A\+DI port value or the smart port value is not within its valid range (A\+DI port\+: 1-\/8, \textquotesingle{}a\textquotesingle{}-\/\textquotesingle{}h\textquotesingle{}, or \textquotesingle{}A\textquotesingle{}-\/\textquotesingle{}H\textquotesingle{}; smart port\+: 1-\/21). E\+A\+D\+D\+R\+I\+N\+U\+SE -\/ The port is not configured as an ultrasonic


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em ult} & The adi\+\_\+ultrasonic\+\_\+t object from \mbox{\hyperlink{group__c-adi_ga2bd844aa49e221c1e68c0b94d148c3b4}{adi\+\_\+ultrasonic\+\_\+init()}} to read\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
The distance to the nearest object in m$^\wedge$-\/4 (10000 indicates 1 meter), measured from the sensor\textquotesingle{}s mounting points. 
\end{DoxyReturn}
\mbox{\Hypertarget{namespacepros_1_1c_aa9c9828dbd73694315c1b1cf5cdb59d8}\label{namespacepros_1_1c_aa9c9828dbd73694315c1b1cf5cdb59d8}}

{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{namespacepros_1_1c_a628d2ba74a77b5d590e4b865e3f4a7aa}{ext\+\_\+adi\+\_\+ultrasonic\+\_\+t}} pros\+::c\+::ext\+\_\+adi\+\_\+ultrasonic\+\_\+init (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{uint8\+\_\+t}]{smart\+\_\+port,  }\item[{uint8\+\_\+t}]{adi\+\_\+port\+\_\+ping,  }\item[{uint8\+\_\+t}]{adi\+\_\+port\+\_\+echo }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Creates an ultrasonic object and configures the specified ports accordingly. 

This function uses the following values of errno when an error state is reached\+: E\+N\+X\+IO -\/ Either the A\+DI port value or the smart port value is not within its valid range (A\+DI port\+: 1-\/8, \textquotesingle{}a\textquotesingle{}-\/\textquotesingle{}h\textquotesingle{}, or \textquotesingle{}A\textquotesingle{}-\/\textquotesingle{}H\textquotesingle{}; smart port\+: 1-\/21). E\+A\+D\+D\+R\+I\+N\+U\+SE -\/ The port is not configured as an ultrasonic


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em smart\+\_\+port} & The smart port number that the A\+DI Expander is in \\
\hline
{\em adi\+\_\+port\+\_\+ping} & The port connected to the orange O\+U\+T\+P\+UT cable. This should be in port 1, 3, 5, or 7 (\textquotesingle{}A\textquotesingle{}, \textquotesingle{}C\textquotesingle{}, \textquotesingle{}E\textquotesingle{}, \textquotesingle{}G\textquotesingle{}). \\
\hline
{\em adi\+\_\+port\+\_\+echo} & The port connected to the yellow I\+N\+P\+UT cable. This should be in the next highest port following port\+\_\+ping.\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
An adi\+\_\+ultrasonic\+\_\+t object to be stored and used for later calls to ultrasonic functions 
\end{DoxyReturn}

\index{pros::c@{pros::c}!ext\_adi\_gyro\_get@{ext\_adi\_gyro\_get}}

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{ext\_adi\_gyro\_get()}{ext\_adi\_gyro\_get()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily double pros\+::c\+::ext\+\_\+adi\+\_\+gyro\+\_\+get (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{namespacepros_1_1c_aeb1fda9da4589cd3cd2e9efe5693f308}{ext\+\_\+adi\+\_\+gyro\+\_\+t}}}]{gyro }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Gets the current gyro angle in tenths of a degree. 

Unless a multiplier is applied to the gyro, the return value will be a whole number representing the number of degrees of rotation times 10.

There are 360 degrees in a circle, thus the gyro will return 3600 for one whole rotation.

This function uses the following values of errno when an error state is reached\+: E\+N\+X\+IO -\/ Either the A\+DI port value or the smart port value is not within its valid range (A\+DI port\+: 1-\/8, \textquotesingle{}a\textquotesingle{}-\/\textquotesingle{}h\textquotesingle{}, or \textquotesingle{}A\textquotesingle{}-\/\textquotesingle{}H\textquotesingle{}; smart port\+: 1-\/21). E\+A\+D\+D\+R\+I\+N\+U\+SE -\/ The port is not configured as a gyro


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em gyro} & The adi\+\_\+gyro\+\_\+t object for which the angle will be returned\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
The gyro angle in degrees. 
\end{DoxyReturn}
\mbox{\Hypertarget{namespacepros_1_1c_a62cddb9a1858256f0fa03effc89ddb20}\label{namespacepros_1_1c_a62cddb9a1858256f0fa03effc89ddb20}} 
\index{pros::c@{pros::c}!ext\_adi\_gyro\_init@{ext\_adi\_gyro\_init}}

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{ext\_adi\_gyro\_init()}{ext\_adi\_gyro\_init()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{namespacepros_1_1c_aeb1fda9da4589cd3cd2e9efe5693f308}{ext\+\_\+adi\+\_\+gyro\+\_\+t}} pros\+::c\+::ext\+\_\+adi\+\_\+gyro\+\_\+init (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{uint8\+\_\+t}]{smart\+\_\+port,  }\item[{uint8\+\_\+t}]{adi\+\_\+port,  }\item[{double}]{multiplier }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Initializes a gyroscope on the given port. 

If the given port has not previously been configured as a gyro, then this function starts a 1300 ms calibration period.

It is highly recommended that this function be called from \mbox{\hyperlink{main_8h_a9efe22aaead3a5e936b5df459de02eba}{initialize()}} when the robot is stationary to ensure proper calibration.

This function uses the following values of errno when an error state is reached\+: E\+N\+X\+IO -\/ Either the A\+DI port value or the smart port value is not within its valid range (A\+DI port\+: 1-\/8, \textquotesingle{}a\textquotesingle{}-\/\textquotesingle{}h\textquotesingle{}, or \textquotesingle{}A\textquotesingle{}-\/\textquotesingle{}H\textquotesingle{}; smart port\+: 1-\/21). E\+A\+D\+D\+R\+I\+N\+U\+SE -\/ The port is not configured as a gyro


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em smart\+\_\+port} & The smart port number that the A\+DI Expander is in \\
\hline
{\em adi\+\_\+port} & The A\+DI port to initialize as a gyro (from 1-\/8, \textquotesingle{}a\textquotesingle{}-\/\textquotesingle{}h\textquotesingle{}, \textquotesingle{}A\textquotesingle{}-\/\textquotesingle{}H\textquotesingle{}) \\
\hline
{\em multiplier} & A scalar value that will be multiplied by the gyro heading value supplied by the A\+DI\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
An adi\+\_\+gyro\+\_\+t object containing the given port, or P\+R\+O\+S\+\_\+\+E\+RR if the initialization failed. 
\end{DoxyReturn}
\mbox{\Hypertarget{namespacepros_1_1c_a91d5a238cdf4fcde887bbb88e3a7ecb0}\label{namespacepros_1_1c_a91d5a238cdf4fcde887bbb88e3a7ecb0}}

Gets the current potentiometer angle in tenths of a degree. 

The original potentiometer rotates 250 degrees thus returning an angle between 0-\/250 degrees. Potentiometer V2 rotates 333 degrees thus returning an angle between 0-\/333 degrees.

Get the G\+PS\textquotesingle{}s location relative to the center of turning/origin in meters.

\index{pros::c@{pros::c}!imu\_reset@{imu\_reset}}
\index{imu\_reset@{imu\_reset}!pros::c@{pros::c}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{imu\_reset()}{imu\_reset()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily int32\+\_\+t pros\+::c\+::imu\+\_\+reset (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{uint8\+\_\+t}]{port }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Calibrate I\+MU. 

Calibration takes approximately 2 seconds, but this function only blocks until the I\+MU status flag is set properly to E\+\_\+\+I\+M\+U\+\_\+\+S\+T\+A\+T\+U\+S\+\_\+\+C\+A\+L\+I\+B\+R\+A\+T\+I\+NG, with a minimum blocking time of 5ms.

This function uses the following values of errno when an error state is reached\+: E\+N\+X\+IO -\/ The given value is not within the range of V5 ports (1-\/21). E\+N\+O\+D\+EV -\/ The port cannot be configured as an Inertial Sensor E\+A\+G\+A\+IN -\/ The sensor is already calibrating, or time out setting the status flag.


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em port} & The V5 Inertial Sensor port number from 1-\/21 \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
1 if the operation was successful or P\+R\+O\+S\+\_\+\+E\+RR if the operation failed setting errno. 
\end{DoxyReturn}
\mbox{\Hypertarget{namespacepros_1_1c_a73029aa0aa910f9b740ffe6def05e830}\label{namespacepros_1_1c_a73029aa0aa910f9b740ffe6def05e830}} 
\index{pros::c@{pros::c}!imu\_set\_data\_rate@{imu\_set\_data\_rate}}
\index{imu\_set\_data\_rate@{imu\_set\_data\_rate}!pros::c@{pros::c}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{imu\_set\_data\_rate()}{imu\_set\_data\_rate()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily int32\+\_\+t pros\+::c\+::imu\+\_\+set\+\_\+data\+\_\+rate (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{uint8\+\_\+t}]{port,  }\item[{uint32\+\_\+t}]{rate }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Set the Inertial Sensor\textquotesingle{}s refresh interval in milliseconds. 

The rate may be specified in increments of 5ms, and will be rounded down to the nearest increment. The minimum allowable refresh rate is 5ms. The default rate is 10ms.

As values are copied into the shared memory buffer only at 10ms intervals, setting this value to less than 10ms does not mean that you can poll the sensor\textquotesingle{}s values any faster. However, it will guarantee that the data is as recent as possible.

This function uses the following values of errno when an error state is reached\+: E\+N\+X\+IO -\/ The given value is not within the range of V5 ports (1-\/21). E\+N\+O\+D\+EV -\/ The port cannot be configured as an Inertial Sensor E\+A\+G\+A\+IN -\/ The sensor is still calibrating


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em port} & The V5 Inertial Sensor port number from 1-\/21 \\
\hline
{\em rate} & The data refresh interval in milliseconds \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
1 if the operation was successful or P\+R\+O\+S\+\_\+\+E\+RR if the operation failed, setting errno. 
\end{DoxyReturn}
\mbox{\Hypertarget{namespacepros_1_1c_aa44bc46059f8aca47f3317320f1cd5bc}\label{namespacepros_1_1c_aa44bc46059f8aca47f3317320f1cd5bc}} 
\index{pros::c@{pros::c}!imu\_get\_rotation@{imu\_get\_rotation}}
\index{imu\_get\_rotation@{imu\_get\_rotation}!pros::c@{pros::c}}

{\footnotesize\ttfamily double pros\+::c\+::imu\+\_\+get\+\_\+rotation (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{uint8\+\_\+t}]{port }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Get the total number of degrees the Inertial Sensor has spun about the z-\/axis. 

This value is theoretically unbounded. Clockwise rotations are represented with positive degree values, while counterclockwise rotations are represented with negative ones.

This function uses the following values of errno when an error state is reached\+: E\+N\+X\+IO -\/ The given value is not within the range of V5 ports (1-\/21). E\+N\+O\+D\+EV -\/ The port cannot be configured as an Inertial Sensor E\+A\+G\+A\+IN -\/ The sensor is still calibrating


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em port} & The V5 Inertial Sensor port number from 1-\/21 \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
The degree value or P\+R\+O\+S\+\_\+\+E\+R\+R\+\_\+F if the operation failed, setting errno. 
\end{DoxyReturn}

\index{pros::c@{pros::c}!link\_init@{link\_init}}
\index{link\_init@{link\_init}!pros::c@{pros::c}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{link\_init()}{link\_init()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily uint32\+\_\+t pros\+::c\+::link\+\_\+init (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{uint8\+\_\+t}]{port,  }\item[{const char $\ast$}]{link\+\_\+id,  }\item[{link\+\_\+type\+\_\+e\+\_\+t}]{type }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Initializes a link on a radio port, with an indicated type. 

There might be a 1 to 2 second delay from when this function is called to when the link is initializes.

This function uses the following values of errno when an error state is reached\+: E\+N\+X\+IO -\/ The given value is not within the range of V5 ports (1-\/21). E\+N\+O\+D\+EV -\/ The port cannot be configured as a radio. E\+N\+X\+IO -\/ The sensor is still calibrating, or no link is connected via the radio.


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em port} & The port of the radio for the intended link. \\
\hline
{\em link\+\_\+id} & Unique link ID in the form of a string, needs to be different from other links in the area. \\
\hline
{\em type} & Indicates whether the radio link on the brain is a transmitter or reciever, with the transmitter having double the transmitting bandwidth as the recieving end (1040 bytes/s vs 520 bytes/s).\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
P\+R\+O\+S\+\_\+\+E\+RR if initialization fails, 1 if the initialization succeeds. 
\end{DoxyReturn}
\mbox{\Hypertarget{namespacepros_1_1c_a63e9104523a080995babfd88712bc756}\label{namespacepros_1_1c_a63e9104523a080995babfd88712bc756}}

Initializes a link on a radio port, with an indicated type and the ability for vexlink to override the controller radio. 

There might be a 1 to 2 second delay from when this function is called to when the link is initializes.

This function uses the following values of errno when an error state is reached\+: E\+N\+X\+IO -\/ The given value is not within the range of V5 ports (1-\/21). E\+N\+O\+D\+EV -\/ The port cannot be configured as a radio. E\+N\+X\+IO -\/ The sensor is still calibrating, or no link is connected via the radio.


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em port} & The port of the radio for the intended link. \\
\hline
{\em link\+\_\+id} & Unique link ID in the form of a string, needs to be different from other links in the area. \\
\hline
{\em type} & Indicates whether the radio link on the brain is a transmitter or reciever, with the transmitter having double the transmitting bandwidth as the recieving end (1040 bytes/s vs 520 bytes/s).\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
P\+R\+O\+S\+\_\+\+E\+RR if initialization fails, 1 if the initialization succeeds. 
\end{DoxyReturn}

Send raw serial data through vexlink. 

This function uses the following values of errno when an error state is reached\+: E\+N\+X\+IO -\/ The given value is not within the range of V5 ports (1-\/21). E\+N\+O\+D\+EV -\/ The port cannot be configured as a radio. E\+N\+X\+IO -\/ The sensor is still calibrating, or no link is connected via the radio. E\+B\+U\+SY -\/ The transmitter buffer is still busy with a previous transmission, and there is no room in the F\+I\+FO buffer (queue) to transmit the data. E\+I\+N\+V\+AL -\/ The data given is N\+U\+LL

\hline
\end{DoxyParams}

P\+R\+O\+S\+\_\+\+E\+RR if port is not a link, and the successfully transmitted data size if it succeeded. 
\end{DoxyReturn}

 \mbox{\Hypertarget{namespacepros_1_1c_ae116783bc7e5a65b336d8ce2972a720f}\label{namespacepros_1_1c_ae116783bc7e5a65b336d8ce2972a720f}} 
\index{pros::c@{pros::c}!\_\_attribute\_\_@{\_\_attribute\_\_}}
\index{\_\_attribute\_\_@{\_\_attribute\_\_}!pros::c@{pros::c}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{\_\_attribute\_\_()}{\_\_attribute\_\_()}\hspace{0.1cm}{\footnotesize\ttfamily [2/2]}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily motor\+\_\+pid\+\_\+full\+\_\+s\+\_\+t \+\_\+\+\_\+attribute\+\_\+\+\_\+ (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{(deprecated(\char`\"{}Changing these values is not supported by V\+EX and may lead to permanent motor damage.\char`\"{}))}]{ }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Takes in floating point values and returns a properly formatted pid struct. 

Gets the velocity P\+ID that was set for the motor.

Gets the position P\+ID that was set for the motor.

Sets one of motor\+\_\+pid\+\_\+full\+\_\+s\+\_\+t for the motor.

Sets one of motor\+\_\+pid\+\_\+s\+\_\+t for the motor.

The motor\+\_\+pid\+\_\+s\+\_\+t struct is in 4.\+4 format, i.\+e. 0x20 is 2.\+0, 0x21 is 2.\+0625, etc. This function will convert the floating point values to the nearest 4.\+4 value.

This function uses the following values of errno when an error state is reached\+: E\+N\+X\+IO -\/ The given value is not within the range of V5 ports (1-\/21). E\+N\+O\+D\+EV -\/ The port cannot be configured as a motor


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em kf} & The feedforward constant \\
\hline
{\em kp} & The proportional constant \\
\hline
{\em ki} & The integral constant \\
\hline
{\em kd} & The derivative constant\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
A motor\+\_\+pid\+\_\+s\+\_\+t struct formatted properly in 4.\+4.
\end{DoxyReturn}
The motor\+\_\+pid\+\_\+s\+\_\+t struct is in 4.\+4 format, i.\+e. 0x20 is 2.\+0, 0x21 is 2.\+0625, etc. This function will convert the floating point values to the nearest 4.\+4 value.

This function uses the following values of errno when an error state is reached\+: E\+N\+X\+IO -\/ The given value is not within the range of V5 ports (1-\/21). E\+N\+O\+D\+EV -\/ The port cannot be configured as a motor


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em kf} & The feedforward constant \\
\hline
{\em kp} & The proportional constant \\
\hline
{\em ki} & The integral constant \\
\hline
{\em kd} & The derivative constant \\
\hline
{\em filter} & A constant used for filtering the profile acceleration \\
\hline
{\em limit} & The integral limit \\
\hline
{\em threshold} & The threshold for determining if a position movement has reached its goal. This has no effect for velocity P\+ID calculations. \\
\hline
{\em loopspeed} & The rate at which the P\+ID computation is run in ms\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
A motor\+\_\+pid\+\_\+s\+\_\+t struct formatted properly in 4.\+4.
\end{DoxyReturn}
This intended to just modify the main P\+ID constants.

Only non-\/zero values of the struct will change the existing motor constants.

\begin{DoxyNote}{Note}
This feature is in beta, it is advised to use caution when modifying the P\+ID values. The motor could be damaged by particularly large constants.
\end{DoxyNote}
This function uses the following values of errno when an error state is reached\+: E\+N\+X\+IO -\/ The given value is not within the range of V5 ports (1-\/21). E\+N\+O\+D\+EV -\/ The port cannot be configured as a motor


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em port} & The V5 port number from 1-\/21 \\
\hline
{\em pid} & The new motor P\+ID constants\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
1 if the operation was successful or P\+R\+O\+S\+\_\+\+E\+RR if the operation failed, setting errno.
\end{DoxyReturn}
Only non-\/zero values of the struct will change the existing motor constants.

\begin{DoxyNote}{Note}
This feature is in beta, it is advised to use caution when modifying the P\+ID values. The motor could be damaged by particularly large constants.
\end{DoxyNote}
This function uses the following values of errno when an error state is reached\+: E\+N\+X\+IO -\/ The given value is not within the range of V5 ports (1-\/21). E\+N\+O\+D\+EV -\/ The port cannot be configured as a motor


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}

\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
1 if the operation was successful or P\+R\+O\+S\+\_\+\+E\+RR if the operation failed, setting errno.
\end{DoxyReturn}
This function will return zero for all of the parameters if the motor\+\_\+set\+\_\+pos\+\_\+pid() or motor\+\_\+set\+\_\+pos\+\_\+pid\+\_\+full() functions have not been used.

This function uses the following values of errno when an error state is reached\+: E\+N\+X\+IO -\/ The given value is not within the range of V5 ports (1-\/21). E\+N\+O\+D\+EV -\/ The port cannot be configured as a motor

Additionally, in an error state all values of the returned struct are set to their negative maximum values.

{\footnotesize\ttfamily int32\+\_\+t pros\+::c\+::rotation\+\_\+set\+\_\+data\+\_\+rate (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{uint8\+\_\+t}]{port,  }\item[{uint32\+\_\+t}]{rate }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Set the \mbox{\hyperlink{classpros_1_1Rotation}{Rotation}} Sensor\textquotesingle{}s refresh interval in milliseconds. 

The rate may be specified in increments of 5ms, and will be rounded down to the nearest increment. The minimum allowable refresh rate is 5ms. The default rate is 10ms.

This function uses the following values of errno when an error state is reached\+: E\+N\+X\+IO -\/ The given value is not within the range of V5 ports (1-\/21). E\+N\+O\+D\+EV -\/ The port cannot be configured as an \mbox{\hyperlink{classpros_1_1Rotation}{Rotation}} Sensor


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em port} & The V5 \mbox{\hyperlink{classpros_1_1Rotation}{Rotation}} Sensor port number from 1-\/21 \\
\hline
{\em rate} & The data refresh interval in milliseconds \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
1 if the operation was successful or P\+R\+O\+S\+\_\+\+E\+RR if the operation failed, setting errno. 
\end{DoxyReturn}

{\footnotesize\ttfamily int32\+\_\+t pros\+::c\+::rotation\+\_\+init\+\_\+reverse (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{uint8\+\_\+t}]{port,  }\item[{bool}]{reverse\+\_\+flag }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Initialize the \mbox{\hyperlink{classpros_1_1Rotation}{Rotation}} Sensor with a reverse flag. 

This function uses the following values of errno when an error state is reached\+: E\+N\+X\+IO -\/ The given value is not within the range of V5 ports (1-\/21). E\+N\+O\+D\+EV -\/ The port cannot be configured as an \mbox{\hyperlink{classpros_1_1Rotation}{Rotation}} Sensor


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em port} & The V5 \mbox{\hyperlink{classpros_1_1Rotation}{Rotation}} Sensor port number from 1-\/21 \\
\hline
{\em reverse\+\_\+flag} & Determines if the \mbox{\hyperlink{classpros_1_1Rotation}{Rotation}} Sensor is reversed or not.\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
1 if the operation was successful or P\+R\+O\+S\+\_\+\+E\+RR if the operation failed, setting errno. 
\end{DoxyReturn}
\mbox{\Hypertarget{namespacepros_1_1c_a8cebefc88493efb298f15e6f47eb7992}\label{namespacepros_1_1c_a8cebefc88493efb298f15e6f47eb7992}}

{\footnotesize\ttfamily int32\+\_\+t pros\+::c\+::rotation\+\_\+get\+\_\+reversed (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{uint8\+\_\+t}]{port }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Get the \mbox{\hyperlink{classpros_1_1Rotation}{Rotation}} Sensor\textquotesingle{}s reversed flag. 

This function uses the following values of errno when an error state is reached\+: E\+N\+X\+IO -\/ The given value is not within the range of V5 ports (1-\/21). E\+N\+O\+D\+EV -\/ The port cannot be configured as an \mbox{\hyperlink{classpros_1_1Rotation}{Rotation}} Sensor


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em port} & The V5 \mbox{\hyperlink{classpros_1_1Rotation}{Rotation}} Sensor port number from 1-\/21\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
Boolean value of if the \mbox{\hyperlink{classpros_1_1Rotation}{Rotation}} Sensor\textquotesingle{}s direction is reversed or not or P\+R\+O\+S\+\_\+\+E\+RR if the operation failed, setting errno. 
\end{DoxyReturn}
